 bijepi ke sutron kii maane to bijepi mahasachiv ram madhav se milakar haseeb daraabu ne hi bijepi or pidipi gathbandhan sarkaar kii niv rakhi thi

 lekin pidipi hameshaa se kashmir ko raajnneetik samasya maan karpakistanke saath baatcheet karke hi kashmir samasya kaa hal ho isaki maang karti he

 pichley ek saal main jis tarah se aatankwaadiyon ke encounter ko lekar, major aditya maamle yaa isi tarah ke anya maamalon main mukhyamantri mahabuuba mufti yaa pidipi ke netao ke bayaan aaye hai usase bijepi pehle se hi aahat thi

 isiilie rajya bijepi netaaon ko dilli bulaayaa gaya he

 bijepi ke is gathbandhan ke sabhi pahaluon par vichaar kar rahaa he

 isamen jin chaar vyapam adhikariyon ke naam shaamil kiye gaye hai, unamem tatkaaleen vyapam diarector pankaj trivedi, tatkaaleen senior system enelist nitin mohindra, tatkaaleen dipti system enelist ajay kumaar sen or tatkaaleen programmer sike mishra shaamil hai

 tamilnadu kii sattarudh party ediemke ke ek saansad ne kaha he ki jo koi mukhyamantri jayalalita ke swasthya ke bare main baat karegaa, uski jubaan kaat lee jaaegi
 Party MP from Namakkal PR Sundaram made this comment on the statement by m Karunanidhi, leader of the opposition party DMK, in which Karunanidhi said that since Jayalalithaa is ill, she should step down
 sundaram ne kaha, karunanidhi chaahate hai ki ammaa ko aaraam karnaa chahie
 what is your age? He is 93 years old and says he wants to live a hundred years
 vah apane beton ko shakti hastantarit nahin karnaa chaahate hai
 As an MP i must remain restrained, but if a revolutionary leader says anything about Amma, her tongue will be cut off
 tippaniyan Earlier this month, Jayalalithaa was away from work for about 10 days, after which the speculation market started to heat up and several comments came from opposition parties
 ek ore jahaan diemke ne kaha he ki 67-varshiya jayalalita ko mukhyamantri kaa pad chhod dena chahie, vahiin congress netaa iwikees elangowan ne maang kii he ki sarkaar ko yah saaf karnaa chahie ki kya vah (jayalalita) aswasth hai
 Chief Minister Jayalalithaa returned to work on 15 July
 unki party ne in khabaron kaa khandan kiya he ki mukhyamantri liver transplant karaane ke liye videsh jane kaa kaarykram bana rahi hai or aisi khabaron ko vipakshi diemke kii badale kii sajeesh qaraar diya he
 Jayalalithaa was sworn in as an MLA on July 4 after winning by a record number of votes in the assembly by-election
 namakkal se party saansad piaar sundaram ne vipakshi party diemke ke netaa em karunanidhi ke us bayaan par yah tippanee kii, jisamen karunanidhi ne kaha tha ki chunki jayalalita biimaar hai, isliye unhen pad chhod dena chahie
 Sundaram said, Karunanidhi wants Amma to rest
 aapaki umr kya he? vah 93 saal ke hai or kehete hai ki vah sau saal jeena chaahate hai
 He does not want to transfer power to his sons
 ek saansad ke rup main mujhe sanyamit rahanaa chahie, lekin agar koi krantikari netaa ammaa ke bare main kuch kahata he, to uski jubaan kaat lee jaaegi
 The comments is maheene kii shuruyaat main jayalalita kareeb 10 dinon tak kaam se dur raheen, jiske baad atakalon kaa bazaar garm ho gaya or vipakshi partiyon kii ore se kai tippaniyan saamne ain
 While the DMK has said that 67-year-old Jayalalithaa should step down as chief minister, Congress leader EVKS Ilangovan has demanded that the government should make it clear whether she (jayalalithaa) is unwell

 a post shared by Tiger Shroff (@tigerjackieshroff) on Sep 27, 2018 at 1:56am PDT Today is Mahavir Jayanti
 mahavir jayanti (mahavira Jayanti) har saal puri duniya main bade hi harshollas ke saath manaai jaati he
 Shukla Trayodashi is celebrated in the month of Chaitra, the birthday of Lord Mahavir (swami Mahavira), the 24th Tirthankara of Jainism
 hinsa, pashubali, jaat-paat kaa bhed-bhav jis yug main bad gaya, usee yug main bhagwaan mahavir (swami Mahavir) kaa janm hua
 He taught the world the truth, non-violence
 mahavir ne ahimsa ko sarvopari bataaya or jain dharm ke panchasheel siddhant die
 These include non-violence, truth, aparigraha, astya and brahmacharya
 unhone anekantwaad, syadawaad or aparigrah jaise adbhut siddhant die
 The self-righteousness of Lord Mahavir was the same for every soul of the world
 duniya kii sabhi aatma ek-si hai isliye ham dusron ke prati vahi vichaar evam vyavhaar rakhen jo hamen swayan ko pasand ho
 This is Mahavira's principle of 'live and let live'
 bataa den ki jain dharm ke anuyaayiyon ke liye mahavir jayanti (mahavir Jayanti) kaa vishesh mahatv he
 It is one of their major festivals
 mahavir jayanti ko mahavir swami janm kalyanak ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 The idols of Mahavir are anointed in Jain temples on the day of Mahavir Jayanti
 iske baad murti ko ek rath par bithakar juluus nikaala jaataa he
 Followers of Jainism participate extensively in this journey
